Float:PlayerTheoreticAngle(Player)
{
new Float:X;
new Float:Y;
new Float:Z;
GetVehiclePos(GetPlayerVehicleID(Player),X,Y,Z);
new Float:NewX;
if(X > PlayerPositionX[Player]) NewX = X - PlayerPositionX[Player];
if(X < PlayerPositionX[Player]) NewX = PlayerPositionX[Player] - X;
new Float:NewY;
if(Y > PlayerPositionY[Player]) NewY = Y - PlayerPositionY[Player];
if(Y < PlayerPositionY[Player]) NewY = PlayerPositionY[Player] - Y;
new Float:Sinus;
new Float:Cosinus;
Cosinus = floatsqroot(floatpower(floatabs(floatsub(X,PlayerPositionX[Player])),2) + floatpower(floatabs(floatsub(Y,PlayerPositionY[Player])),2));
new Float:TheoreticAngle;
if(PlayerPositionX[Player] > X && PlayerPositionY[Player] > Y){Sinus = asin(NewX / Cosinus);TheoreticAngle = floatsub(floatsub(floatadd(Sinus,90),floatmul(Sinus,2)),-90.0);}
if(PlayerPositionX[Player] > X && PlayerPositionY[Player] < Y){Sinus = asin(NewX / Cosinus);TheoreticAngle = floatsub(floatadd(Sinus,180),180.0);}
if(PlayerPositionX[Player] < X && PlayerPositionY[Player] < Y){Sinus = acos(NewY / Cosinus);TheoreticAngle = floatsub(floatadd(Sinus,360),floatmul(Sinus,2));}
if(PlayerPositionX[Player] < X && PlayerPositionY[Player] > Y){Sinus = asin(NewX / Cosinus);TheoreticAngle = floatadd(Sinus,180);}
if(TheoreticAngle == 0.0) GetVehicleZAngle(GetPlayerVehicleID(Player),TheoreticAngle);return TheoreticAngle;}
VehicleIsCar(Vehicle){
new Stritreyser[6]={562, 565, 559 ,561, 560, 558};
new Gonochny[13]={429, 541, 415, 480, 434, 494, 502, 503, 411, 506, 451, 555, 477};
new LowRider[7]={536, 575, 534, 567, 535, 576, 412};

new Vantajnyrobochy[18]={499, 498, 609, 524, 532, 578, 406, 573, 455, 588, 403, 423, 414, 443, 515, 514, 531, 456};
new Lehkivantajivku[13]={459, 422, 282, 530, 418, 572, 582, 413, 440, 543, 583, 478, 554};
new Dlyarozvag[12]={568, 424, 504, 457, 483, 508, 500, 444, 556, 557, 471, 495};
new Dlyatransportuvannya[9]={485, 431, 438, 437, 574, 420, 525, 408, 552};
new Derjavni[14]={416, 433, 427, 490, 528, 544, 470, 596, 697, 598, 599, 432, 428, 601};
new Pobuti[2]={604, 605};
new modelid=GetVehicleModel(Vehicle);
new i;
for(i=0;i<6;i++){if(Stritreyser[i]==modelid) return 1;}
for(i=0;i<13;i++){if(Gonochny[i]==modelid) return 1;}
for(i=0;i<7;i++){if(LowRider[i]==modelid) return 1;}
for(i=0;i<19;i++){if(Dvohdverny[i]==modelid) return 1;}
for(i=0;i<19;i++){if(Hcoturudverny[i]==modelid) return 1;}
for(i=0;i<8;i++){if(Djeeps[i]==modelid) return 1;}
for(i=0;i<4;i++){if(Potujny[i]==modelid) return 1;}
for(i=0;i<18;i++){if(Vantajnyrobochy[i]==modelid) return 1;}
for(i=0;i<13;i++){if(Lehkivantajivku[i]==modelid) return 1;}
for(i=0;i<12;i++){if(Dlyarozvag[i]==modelid) return 1;}
for(i=0;i<9;i++){if(Dlyatransportuvannya[i]==modelid) return 1;}
for(i=0;i<14;i++){if(Derjavni[i]==modelid) return 1;}
for(i=0;i<2;i++){if(Pobuti[i]==modelid) return 1;}
return 0;
}

stock VehicleSpeed(Vehicle)
{
new Float:X;
new Float:Y;
new Float:Z;
GetVehicleVelocity(Vehicle,X,Y,Z);
new Float:Speed;
Speed = floatsqroot(floatpower(floatabs(X),2.0) + floatpower(floatabs(Y),2.0) + floatpower(floatabs(Z),2.0)) * 110.0;
return floatround(Speed);
}

public OnPlayerEnterDynamicArea(playerid, areaid)
{
if (areaid == zoneid)
{
ZoneTimer[playerid] = SetTimerEx("StartZoneAudio", 6000, false, "i", playerid);// запускаємо таймер 6 сек
}
return 1;
}

public OnPlayerLeaveDynamicArea(playerid, areaid)
{
if (areaid == zoneid)
{

if (ZoneTimer[playerid])// скасовуємо таймер
{
KillTimer(ZoneTimer[playerid]);
ZoneTimer[playerid] = 0;
}
StopAudioStreamForPlayer(playerid);// зупиняємо музику
PlayAudioStreamForPlayer(playerid, "OFF");
}
return 1;
}

public OnGameModeExit()
{
if(restrest == 0){
KillTimer(fivesectimer);
KillTimer(restart);
KillTimer(autorepaircar);
KillTimer(onsectimer);
KillTimer(minsertimer);
KillTimer(timer200);
KillTimer(timpolsec);
KillTimer(ServerTimerOne);
KillTimer(ServerTimerTwo);
}
for(new Player; Player < GetMaxPlayers(); Player++)
{
TextDrawDestroy(ServerTextDrawThree[Player]);
TextDrawDestroy(ServerTextDrawFour[Player]);
TextDrawDestroy(ServerTextDrawFive[Player]);
}
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
TextDrawHideForPlayer(i, TScore[i]);
TextDrawDestroy(TScore[i]);

if(mapiconid[i] != -600)
{
DestroyDynamicMapIcon(mapiconid[i]);
}
mapiconid[i] = -600;
if(IsPlayerConnected(i)){
PlayKick(i);}}
}
public OnPlayerRequestClass(playerid, classid)
{
TogglePlayerSpectating(playerid, 0);
TextDrawHideForPlayer(playerid, Wasted1);
PlayerPlaySound(playerid, 5202, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
SetPlayerFacingAngle(playerid, 267.5125);
SetPlayerPos(playerid, 2035.9551,1007.5748,10.8203);
SetPlayerCameraPos(playerid, 2041.4668,1007.2496,10.6719);
SetPlayerCameraLookAt(playerid, 2035.9551,1007.5748,10.8203);
ApplyAnimation(playerid,"PED", "WALK_drunk",9.9,9,9,9,9,9);

return 1;
}
public OnPlayerConnect(playerid)
{
new ip[64];
new string[256];

if(IsPlayerConnected(playerid))
{
new ololo[6][128];
getdate(timedata[2], timedata[3], timedata[4]);
//SetWorldTime(timedata[0]);

gettime(timedata[0], timedata[1]);
//GetPlayerTime(playerid, timedata[0], timedata[1]);

GetPlayerIp(playerid,ip,sizeof(ip));
new File = ini_openFile("zabaneni.ini");ini_getString(File,ip,string);ini_closeFile(File);
split(string, ololo, ',');ddd[playerid] = strval(ololo[0]);mmm[playerid] = strval(ololo[1]);yyy[playerid] = strval(ololo[2]);aaa[playerid] = strval(ololo[3]);bbb[playerid] = strval(ololo[4]);ccc[playerid] = strval(ololo[5]);

if(ddd[playerid] != 0 && mmm[playerid] != 0 && yyy[playerid] != 0)
{
if(ddd[playerid] > timedata[4] && mmm[playerid] == timedata[3] && yyy[playerid] == timedata[2])
{
TogglePlayerSpectating(playerid, 1);
format(string,sizeof(string),"\n{FFFFFF} -----   {00FFFF}Ви тимчасово забаненi на цьому серверi   {FFFFFF}----- \n\n {FF00FF}Дата видачi бану :   {FFD700}%02d/%02d/%04d\
\n\n {00FF00}Доступ буде вiдновлений :   {FFD700}%02d/%02d/%04d\n\n",aaa[playerid],bbb[playerid],ccc[playerid],ddd[playerid],mmm[playerid],yyy[playerid]);
ShowPlayerDialog(playerid,2,0,"      {FF0000}В доступi вiдмовлено",string,"","");
ClearChat(playerid, 0);

GameTextForPlayer(player[playerid], "~r~---  вас було забанено  ---", 30000, 1);
return 1;
}
if(mmm[playerid] > timedata[3] && yyy[playerid] == timedata[2])
{
TogglePlayerSpectating(playerid, 1);
format(string,sizeof(string),"\n{FFFFFF} -----   {00FFFF}Ви тимчасово забаненi на цьому серверi   {FFFFFF}----- \n\n {FF00FF}Дата видачi бану :   {FFD700}%02d/%02d/%04d\
\n\n {00FF00}Доступ буде вiдновлений :   {FFD700}%02d/%02d/%04d\n\n",aaa[playerid],bbb[playerid],ccc[playerid],ddd[playerid],mmm[playerid],yyy[playerid]);

SetTimerEx("PlayKick", 300, 0, "playerid", playerid);

GameTextForPlayer(player[playerid], "~r~---  вас було забанено  ---", 30000, 1);
return 1;
}
if(yyy[playerid] > timedata[2])
{
TogglePlayerSpectating(playerid, 1);
format(string,sizeof(string),"\n{FFFFFF} -----   {00FFFF}Ви тимчасово забаненi на цьому серверi   {FFFFFF}----- \n\n {FF00FF}Дата видачi бану :   {FFD700}%02d/%02d/%04d\
\n\n {00FF00}Доступ буде вiдновлений :   {FFD700}%02d/%02d/%04d\n\n",aaa[playerid],bbb[playerid],ccc[playerid],ddd[playerid],mmm[playerid],yyy[playerid]);

return 1;
}
}

{

\n{00FF00}Ви вже зареєстрованi на нашому серверi.\

\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n{00FFFF}Щоб увiйти в акаунт, введiть свiй пароль:", "{00FF00}Увiйти", "");

}
else
{

}
public OnPlayerDisconnect(playerid, reason)
{
StopAudioStreamForPlayer(playerid);
TextDrawHideForPlayer(playerid,ServerTextDrawThree[playerid]);
TextDrawHideForPlayer(playerid,ServerTextDrawFour[playerid]);
TextDrawHideForPlayer(playerid,ServerTextDrawFive[playerid]);
TextDrawSetString(ServerTextDrawThree[playerid]," ");
TextDrawSetString(ServerTextDrawFour[playerid]," ");
TextDrawSetString(ServerTextDrawFive[playerid]," ");
PlayerMoney[playerid] = 0;
PlayerScore[playerid] = 0;
PlayerCombo[playerid] = 1;
PlayerPositionX[playerid] = 0.0;
PlayerPositionY[playerid] = 0.0;
PlayerPositionZ[playerid] = 0.0;
KillTimer(PlayerTimerOne[playerid]);
KillTimer(PlayerInfo[playerid][pAntiSKTmr]);
if(TextdrawActive[playerid] == 1)
{
TextDrawHideForPlayer(playerid, TextDraw[playerid]);
TextDrawDestroy(TextDraw[playerid]);
}
new string[256];
new pname[MAX_PLAYER_NAME];
GetPlayerName(playerid, pname, sizeof(pname));
format(string,sizeof(string),"* %s [%d] вийшов з сервера.",RealName[playerid],playerid);
switch(reason)
{
case 0: format(string,sizeof(string),"%s (вилiт)",string);
case 1: format(string,sizeof(string),"%s (вийшов)",string);
case 2: format(string,sizeof(string),"%s (кiк/бан)",string);
}
SendClientMessageToAll(0x00FF00FF, string);
format(string,sizeof(string),"* Гравець %s [%d] вийшов з сервера.",RealName[playerid],playerid);
switch(reason)
{
case 0: format(string,sizeof(string),"%s (вилiт)",string);
case 1: format(string,sizeof(string),"%s (вийшов)",string);
case 2: format(string,sizeof(string),"%s (кiк/бан)",string);
}
if(mapiconid[playerid] != -600)
{
DestroyDynamicMapIcon(mapiconid[playerid]);
}
mapiconid[playerid] = -600;

new Float:X, Float:Y, Float:Z;
new Float:Xc, Float:Yc, Float:Zc, Float:ras;
GetPlayerPos(playerid, X, Y, Z);
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
{
if(admper1[i] == playerid)
{
TogglePlayerSpectating(i, 0);
admper6[i] = 0;
ShowPlayerDialog(i, 2, 0 ,"{FFFF00}iнформацiя.", "Спостереження було автоматично вимкнене !\
\n( гравець, за яким Ви спостерiгали - вийшов з сервера )", "{00FF00}OK", "");
}
GetPlayerPos(i, Xc, Yc, Zc);
new Float:locX, Float:locY, Float:locZ;
locX = X - Xc;
locY = Y - Yc;
locZ = Z - Zc;
if((reason == 0 || reason == 2) && playerid != i &&
(-1000 < locX < 1000 && -1000 < locY < 1000 && -1000 < locZ < 1000))
{
ras = floatsqroot(floatmul(locX, locX) + floatmul(locY, locY) + floatmul(locZ, locZ));
format(string, sizeof(string), "%f", ras);
new dop1;
dop1 = strval(string);
if(reason == 0)
{
format(string, sizeof(string),
"* Краш-монiтор - гравець ''вилетiв'': %s [%d] , гравець поруч: %s [%d] , вiдстань: %d",RealName[playerid], playerid, RealName[i], i, dop1);
}
if(reason == 2)
{
format(string, sizeof(string),
"* Краш-монiтор - гравець ''кiк/бан'': %s [%d] , гравець поруч: %s [%d] , вiдстань: %d",RealName[playerid], playerid, RealName[i], i, dop1);
}
for(new j; j < GetMaxPlayers(); j++)
//for(new j = 0; j < MAX_PLAYERS; j++)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(j))
{
if(plcmonloc[j] == 1 && plcmondist[j] >= dop1)
{
SendClientMessage(j, 0xFF6347FF, string);
}
}
}
}
}
}
for(new j = 0; j < 13; j++)
{
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pPrisonsec] > 0)
{
playweap[playerid][j] = play2weap[playerid][j];
playammo[playerid][j] = play2ammo[playerid][j];
}
else
{
GetPlayerWeaponData(playerid, j, playweap[playerid][j], playammo[playerid][j]);
}
}
OnPlayerSaveA(playerid);
if(idgangsave[playerid] > 0)
{
GangSave(idgangsave[playerid]);
}
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pPrisonsec] > 0)
{
format(string, sizeof(string), "* Гравець %s [%d] вийшов з сервера з %d секундами в'язницi.", RealName[playerid], playerid,
PlayerInfo[playerid][pPrisonsec]);
SendClientMessageToAll(0xFFFF00FF, string);
}
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pMutedsec] > 0)
{
format(string, sizeof(string), "* Гравець %s [%d] вийшов с сервера з %d секундами затику.", RealName[playerid], playerid,
PlayerInfo[playerid][pMutedsec]);
SendClientMessageToAll(0xFFFF00FF, string);
}
TogglePlayerControllable(playerid, 1);
if(neon[playerid][0] != 0) { DestroyObject(neon[playerid][0]); }
if(neon[playerid][1] != 0) { DestroyObject(neon[playerid][1]); }
neon[playerid][0] = 0;
neon[playerid][1] = 0;
neon[playerid][2] = 0;
if(playcar[playerid] != 0)
{
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
if(playcar[playerid] == neon[i][2])
{
DestroyObject(neon[i][0]);
DestroyObject(neon[i][1]);
neon[i][0] = 0;
neon[i][1] = 0;
neon[i][2] = 0;
}
}
DestroyVehicle(playcar[playerid]);
playcar[playerid] = 0;
}

NRadio[playerid] = 0;
StopAudioStreamForPlayer(playerid);
TextDrawHideForPlayer(playerid, TScore[playerid]);

SetPlayerFightingStyle(playerid, FIGHT_STYLE_NORMAL);
moneycontrol[playerid] = 0;
moneycontrol22[playerid] = 0;
DeletePVar(playerid, "MonControl");
scorecontrol[playerid] = 0;
scorecontrol22[playerid] = 0;
DeletePVar(playerid, "ScorControl");
plcmonloc[playerid] = 0;
deathcon[playerid] = 0;
DeletePVar(playerid, "PlSkin");
gPlayerLogged[playerid] = 0;
playspa[playerid] = 0;
dlgcont[playerid] = -600;
countdown[playerid] = -1;
oneminkick[playerid] = 0;
prisoncount[playerid] = 0;
DeletePVar(playerid, "AdmLvl");
DeletePVar(playerid, "PlGLvl");
DeletePVar(playerid, "PlGng");
DeletePVar(playerid, "CComAc0");
DeletePVar(playerid, "CComAc1");
DeletePVar(playerid, "CComAc2");
DeletePVar(playerid, "CComAc3");
DeletePVar(playerid, "CComAc4");
DeletePVar(playerid, "CComAc5");
DeletePVar(playerid, "CComAc6");
DeletePVar(playerid, "CComAc7");
DeletePVar(playerid, "CComAc8");
DeletePVar(playerid, "CComAc9");
DeletePVar(playerid, "CComAc10");
DeletePVar(playerid, "CComAc11");
DeletePVar(playerid, "CComAc12");
DeletePVar(playerid, "CComAc13");
DeletePVar(playerid, "CComAc14");
DeletePVar(playerid, "CComAc15");
strdel(RealName[playerid], 0, MAX_PLAYER_NAME);
dialogadm[playerid] = 0;
dialogcon[playerid] = 0;
functioncon[playerid] = 0;
chatcon[playerid] = 0;
strdel(fbanreason[playerid], 0, 256);
LockSpawn[playerid] = 0;

PlayLock1[0][playerid] = 600;
PlayerInfo[playerid][pMinlog] = 0;
PlayerInfo[playerid][pAdmlive] = 0;
livdop[playerid] = 0;
PlayerInfo[playerid][pAdmin] = 0;
PlayerInfo[playerid][pAdmshad] = 0;
if(SnowONOFF[playerid] == 1)
{
DestroyPlayerObject(playerid, snowobj[playerid]);
SnowONOFF[playerid] = 0;
}
strdel(twoIP[playerid], 0, 64);
strcat(twoIP[playerid], PlayerInfo[playerid][pIPAdr]);
SetTimerEx("ClearIP", 100, 0, "i", playerid);
SetTimerEx("OutOut", 300, 0, "i", playerid);
return 1;
}
forward OutOut(playerid);
public OutOut(playerid)
{
if(idgangsave[playerid] > 0)
{
idgangsave[playerid] = 0;
locper3[playerid] = 0;
while(locper3[playerid] < MAX_PLAYERS)
{
if(PGang[playerid] > 0 && PGang[playerid] == PGang[locper3[playerid]] && playerid != locper3[playerid])
{
idgangsave[locper3[playerid]] = PGang[playerid];
break;
}
locper3[playerid]++;
}
}
idgangsave[playerid] = 0;

PGang[playerid] = 0;
GangLvl[playerid] = 0;
return 1;
}
forward ClearIP(playerid);
public ClearIP(playerid)
{
strdel(twoIP[playerid], 0, 64);
return 1;
}

public OnPlayerSpawn(playerid)
{
if (IsPlayerInDynamicArea(playerid, zoneid))
{
ZoneTimer[playerid] = SetTimerEx("StartZoneAudio", 6000, false, "i", playerid);
}

SetPlayerHealth(playerid, 99999);
PlayerInfo[playerid][pAntiSKTmr] = SetTimerEx("AntiSpawnKill", 10000, 0, "i", playerid);//захист від вбивства на спавні на час
functioncon[playerid]++;
new string[256];
if(deathcon[playerid] == 1)
{
deathcon[playerid] = 0;
}
if(gPlayerLogged[playerid] == 0)
{
format(string,sizeof(string),"* Гравець %s [%d] був кiкнутий - спавн без авторизацiї !", RealName[playerid], playerid);
SendClientMessageToAll(0xFF6347FF, string);
ClearChat(playerid, 0);
SetTimerEx("PlayKick", 300, 0, "i", playerid);
return 1;
}
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pLock] == 1) { return 1; }

if(PlayLock1[0][playerid] != 600 && PlayerInfo[playerid][pPrisonsec] == 0)
{
PlayLock1[1][playerid] = 10;
PlayLock1[2][playerid] = 0;
PlayLock2[0][playerid] = 215.97;
PlayLock2[1][playerid] = 114.45;
PlayLock2[2][playerid] = 999.01;
PlayLock2[3][playerid] = 269.82;
SetCameraBehindPlayer(playerid);
}
else
{
if(admper1[playerid] != 600)
{
new cordz = 0;
if(admper4[playerid] == 3)
{
cordz = 5;
}
admper1[playerid] = 600;
SetPlayerInterior(playerid, admper2[playerid]);
SetPlayerVirtualWorld(playerid, admper3[playerid]);
SetPlayerPos(playerid, TelSpec[playerid][0] + admper4[playerid], TelSpec[playerid][1] + admper4[playerid],
TelSpec[playerid][2] + cordz);
SetCameraBehindPlayer(playerid);
if(mapiconid[playerid] != -600)
{
DestroyDynamicMapIcon(mapiconid[playerid]);
}
mapiconid[playerid] = -600;
}
else
{
new locper = random(18);
if(PGang[playerid] > 0 && strlen(GName[PGang[playerid]]) == 0)
{
PGang[playerid] = 0;
GangLvl[playerid] = 0;
SendClientMessage(playerid, 0xFF0000FF, "Ваша банда була видалена !");
SetPlayerInterior(playerid, 0);
SetPlayerVirtualWorld(playerid, 0);

SetPlayerFacingAngle(playerid, playspaa[locper]);
SetCameraBehindPlayer(playerid);
}
else
{
if(PGang[playerid] > 0 && (GSpawnX[PGang[playerid]] != 0.0 ||
GSpawnY[PGang[playerid]] != 0.0 || GSpawnZ[PGang[playerid]] != 0.0))
{
SetPlayerInterior(playerid, GInter[PGang[playerid]]);
SetPlayerVirtualWorld(playerid, GWorld[PGang[playerid]]);
SetPlayerPos(playerid, GSpawnX[PGang[playerid]], GSpawnY[PGang[playerid]], GSpawnZ[PGang[playerid]]);
SetCameraBehindPlayer(playerid);
}
else
{
SetPlayerInterior(playerid, 0);
SetPlayerVirtualWorld(playerid, 0);
SetPlayerPos(playerid, playspax[locper], playspay[locper], playspaz[locper]);
SetPlayerFacingAngle(playerid, playspaa[locper]);
SetCameraBehindPlayer(playerid);
}
if(playspa[playerid] == 0)
{
SetTimerEx("Logg333", 1000, 0, "i", playerid);
}
}
}
}
if(weapstatplay[playerid] == 0)

for(new i = 0; i < 13; i++)
{

public OnPlayerDeath(playerid, killerid, reason)
{
KillTimer(PlayerInfo[playerid][pAntiSKTmr]);
if(killerid == INVALID_PLAYER_ID)
{
GameTextForPlayer(playerid, "~r~печалька", 3000, 2);
SetPlayerScore(playerid,GetPlayerScore(playerid)-3);
PlayerPlaySound(playerid, 31202, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
StopAudioStreamForPlayer(playerid);
PlayAudioStreamForPlayer(playerid, "http://is.gd/YBvvIb");
}
else
{
GameTextForPlayer(playerid, "~r~замочили", 3000, 2);
SetPVarInt(playerid, "ScorControl", 1);
SetPlayerScore(playerid,GetPlayerScore(playerid)-3);
SetPVarInt(playerid, "MonControl", 1);
GGivePlayerMoney(playerid, -8000);
PlayerPlaySound(playerid, 31202, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
StopAudioStreamForPlayer(playerid);
PlayAudioStreamForPlayer(playerid, "http://is.gd/p82wLX");

GameTextForPlayer(killerid, "~g~+ 8.000 $~n~~y~+ 2 очка", 3000, 1);
SetPVarInt(killerid, "ScorControl", 1);
SetPlayerScore(killerid,GetPlayerScore(killerid)+2);
SetPVarInt(killerid, "MonControl", 1);
GGivePlayerMoney(killerid, 8000);
PlayerPlaySound(killerid, 31205, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
}


functioncon[playerid]++;
deathcon[playerid] = 1;
SendDeathMessage(killerid, playerid, reason);
if(killerid != INVALID_PLAYER_ID)
{
PlayerInfo[killerid][pKills] += 1;
PlayerInfo[playerid][pDeaths] += 1;
}
return 1;
}

forward SendClientMessageEx (playerid, color, const message[]);
public SendClientMessageEx (playerid, color, const message[]){
new length = strlen(message);new outstr[128];new trim;
if (length > 127){
for (new i = 127; i>=0; i--){
trim = i;
if (message[i] == ' ') break;}
if (trim < 64) trim = 127;
strmid (outstr, message, 0, trim, 128);
SendClientMessage (playerid, color, outstr);
strmid (outstr, message, trim, length, 128);
SendClientMessage (playerid, color, outstr);}
else SendClientMessage (playerid, color, message);
return 1;
}
forward SendClientMessageToAllEx (color, const message[]);
public SendClientMessageToAllEx (color, const message[]){
new length = strlen(message);new outstr[128];new trim;
if (length > 127){
for (new i = 127; i>=0; i--){
trim = i;
if (message[i] == ' ') break;}
if (trim < 64) trim = 127;
strmid (outstr, message, 0, trim, 128);
SendClientMessageToAll (color, outstr);
strmid (outstr, message, trim, length, 128);
SendClientMessageToAll (0xE5B884FF,outstr);}
else SendClientMessageToAll (color, message);
return 1;
}
public OnPlayerText(playerid, text[])
{
chatcon[playerid]++;
new string[256];
if(playspa[playerid] == 0)
{
SendClientMessage(playerid,0xFF0000FF," Ви ще не заспавнились, i не можете писати в чат !");
return 0;
}
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pMutedsec] > 0)
{
SendClientMessage(playerid, 0xFF0000FF, "* Ви не можете говорити, Вас заткнули !");
return 0;
}
if(playspa[playerid] == 1 && PGang[playerid] <= 0)
{
SetPlayerChatBubble(playerid, text, 0xFFFFFFFF, 15.0, 6000);
format(string, sizeof(string), "%s {28F90E}[ID:%d]: {E5B884}%s", RealName[playerid], playerid, text);
SendClientMessageToAllEx(ColorPlay[playerid], string);
return 0;
}
if(playspa[playerid] == 1 && PGang[playerid] > 0)
{
SetPlayerChatBubble(playerid, text, 0xFFFFFFFF, 15.0, 6000);
format(string, sizeof(string), "%s  %s {28F90E}[%d]: {E5B884}%s", GName[PGang[playerid]], RealName[playerid],playerid, text);
SendClientMessageToAllEx(GColorDec[PGang[playerid]], string);
return 0;
}
return 1;
}
forward SendAdminMessage(color, string[]);
public SendAdminMessage(color, string[])
{
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
{
if(PlayerInfo[i][pAdmin] >= 1)
{
SendClientMessage(i, color, string);
}
}
}
return 1;
}
strtok(const string[], &index)
{
new length = strlen(string);
while ((index < length) && (string[index] <= ' '))
{
index++;
}

new offset = index;
new result[30];
while ((index < length) && (string[index] > ' ') && ((index - offset) < (sizeof(result) - 1)))
{
result[index - offset] = string[index];
index++;
}
result[index - offset] = EOS;
return result;
}
public OnPlayerCommandText(playerid, cmdtext[])
{
chatcon[playerid]++;
new idx;
idx = 0;
new string[256];
new strdln[1024];
new akk[64], ssss[256], igkey[64], tdreg[64], adrip[64];
new cmd[128];
new tmp[128];
cmd = strtok(cmdtext, idx);
if(playspa[playerid] == 0)
{
SendClientMessage(playerid, 0xFF0000FF, " Ви ще не заспавнились !");
return 1;
}
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pMutedsec] == 0)
{
}
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pMutedsec] > 0)
{
}
if(strcmp(cmd, "/spawn", true) == 0 && playspa[playerid] == 0)
{
SendClientMessage(playerid,0x00FF00FF," Ви заспавнились !");
if(IsPlayerInAnyVehicle(playerid))
{
new Float:x, Float:y, Float:z;
GetPlayerPos(playerid,x,y,z);
SetPlayerPos(playerid,x,y,z+5);
SetTimerEx("SecSpaDop", 300, 0, "i", playerid);
}
else
{
OnPlayerSpawn(playerid);
}
return 1;
}
/*if(strcmp(cmd, "/хуй", true) == 0)
{
GameTextForAll("~n~~n~~r~краш сервера по запросу~n~~n~~r~краш сервера по запросу~n~~n~~r~краш сервера по запросу~n~~n~~n~~y~SERVER",60000,6);
SendClientMessageToAll(0xFF0000FF, " УВАГА ! Через 10 секунд сервер впаде !");
restart = SetTimer("RestartS", 10000, 1);
return true;
}*/

if(strcmp(cmd, "/me", true) == 0)
{
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pMutedsec] > 0)
{
SendClientMessage(playerid, 0xFFD700FF, "***** Ви не можете писати, у вас бан чату !");
return 1;
}
new pname[MAX_PLAYER_NAME];
GetPlayerName(playerid, pname, sizeof(pname));
new length = strlen(cmdtext);
while ((idx < length) && (cmdtext[idx] <= ' '))
{
idx++;
}
new offset = idx;
new result[128];
while ((idx < length) && ((idx - offset) < (sizeof(result) - 1)))
{
result[idx - offset] = cmdtext[idx];
idx++;
}
result[idx - offset] = EOS;
if(!strlen(result)) return     SendClientMessage(playerid, 0x0000FFFF, "***** Використовуйте: /me [дiя]");
format(string, sizeof(string), "%s %s", pname, result);
ProxDetector(60.0, playerid, string, 0xDD90FFFF, 0xDD90FFFF, 0xDD90FFFF, 0xDD90FFFF, 0xDD90FFFF);
return 1;
}


if(!strcmp(cmdtext, "/nik", true))
{
if(Glow[playerid] == 0)
{
Glow[playerid] = 1;
SendClientMessage(playerid,0x0000FFFF, "***Рiзнокольоровий нiк {00FF00}увiмкнено");
return 1;
}
else if(Glow[playerid] == 1)
{
Glow[playerid] = 0;
SendClientMessage(playerid,0x0000FFFF, "***Рiзнокольоровий нiк {FF0000}вимкнено");
return 1;
}
}

if(strcmp(cmd, "/iznas", true) == 0)
{
tmp = strtok(cmdtext,idx);
new otherplayer = strval(tmp);
if(GetDistanceBetweenPlayers(playerid, otherplayer) > 3) return SendClientMessage(playerid, 0xFFD700FF, " *****  Ви надто далеко!");
if(otherplayer == playerid) return SendClientMessage(playerid, 0xFFD700FF, " *****  Ви не можете згвалтувати самого себе");

case 1: format(string, sizeof(string), "{FF3F3F}%s", result);
case 2: format(string, sizeof(string), "{FF3F00}%s", result);
case 3: format(string, sizeof(string), "{BF3F00}%s", result);

case 11: format(string, sizeof(string), "{00BFFF}%s", result);
case 12: format(string, sizeof(string), "{3F3FFF}%s", result);
case 13: format(string, sizeof(string), "{0000FF}%s", result);
case 14: format(string, sizeof(string), "{7F3FFF}%s", result);
case 15: format(string, sizeof(string), "{7F00FF}%s", result);
case 16: format(string, sizeof(string), "{FF00FF}%s", result);
case 17: format(string, sizeof(string), "{7F7F7F}%s", result);
case 18: format(string, sizeof(string), "{FFFFFF}%s", result);
case 19: format(string, sizeof(string), "{000000}%s", result);
}

tmp = strtok(cmdtext, idx);
level = strval(tmp);
tmp = strtok(cmdtext, idx);
if(!strlen(tmp))
{
summ1 = 0;
}
else
{
summ1 = 1;
summ2 = strval(tmp);
}
if(IsPlayerConnected(para1))
{
if(gPlayerLogged[para1] == 0)
{
SendClientMessage(playerid, 0xFF0000FF, " Обраний гравець ще не залогiнився !");
return 1;
}
if(level < 0 || level > 13)
{
SendClientMessage(playerid, 0xFF0000FF, " Рiвень адмiна повинен бути вiд 0 до 13 !");
return 1;
}
dopper = PlayerInfo[para1][pAdmin];
if(dopper == level)
{
SendClientMessage(playerid, 0xFF0000FF, " У гравця вже є обираємий рiвень адмiна !");
return 1;
}
PlayerInfo[para1][pAdmin] = level;
if(PlayerInfo[para1][pAdmin] == 0)
{
PlayerInfo[para1][pAdmshad] = 0;
format(string, sizeof(string), " *** Адмiн %s зняв адмiнку з гравця %s .", RealName[playerid], RealName[para1]);
SendAdminMessage(0xFF0000FF, string);
format(string, sizeof(string), " *** Адмiн %s зняв з Вас адмiнку.", RealName[playerid]);
SendClientMessage(para1, 0xFF0000FF, string);
if(summ1 == 1 && summ2 != GGetPlayerMoney(para1))
{
SetPVarInt(para1, "MonControl", 1);
ResetPlayerMoney(para1);
GGivePlayerMoney(para1, summ2);
format(string, sizeof(string), " *** Особистий рахунок гравця %s було змiнено на: %d $ .", RealName[para1],
GGetPlayerMoney(para1));
SendAdminMessage(0xFF0000FF, string);
format(string, sizeof(string), " *** Ваш особистий рахунок було змiнено на: %d $ .", GGetPlayerMoney(para1));
SendClientMessage(para1, 0xFF0000FF, string);
}
}
else
{
format(string, sizeof(string), " *** Адмiн %s дав гравцю %s адмiнку %d рiвня.", RealName[playerid],
RealName[para1], level);
SendAdminMessage(0xFFFF00FF, string);
}
if(PlayerInfo[para1][pAdmin] >= 7 && dopper <= 6)
{
PlayerInfo[para1][pAdmlive] = 1;
SendClientMessage(para1, 0x00FF00FF, " Безсмертя увiмкнено.");
}
if(PlayerInfo[para1][pAdmin] <= 6 && dopper >= 7)
{
PlayerInfo[para1][pAdmlive] = 0;
SendClientMessage(para1, 0xFF0000FF, " Безсмертя вимкнено.");
}
if(PlayerInfo[para1][pAdmin] >= 1 && dopper == 0)
{
SendClientMessage(para1, 0xFF0000FF, "* Рекомендацiя: В цiлях безпеки i захисту свого (АДМiНiСТРАТИВНОГО)");
SendClientMessage(para1, 0xFF0000FF, "* акаунта - змiнiть свiй пароль !!! I НЕ використовуйте пароль вiд свого");
SendClientMessage(para1, 0xFF0000FF, "* адмiнiстративного акаунта на iнших серверах !!!");
}
}
else
{
SendClientMessage(playerid, 0xFF0000FF, " Такого [iд гравця] на серверi немає !");
}
}
else
{
SendClientMessage(playerid, 0xFF0000FF, " У Вас немає прав на використання цiєї команди !");
}
return 1;
}
return 0;
}

public OnPlayerEnterVehicle(playerid, vehicleid, ispassenger)
{
if(Death[playerid] == 1){RemovePlayerFromVehicle(playerid);}
return 1;
}

public OnPlayerExitVehicle(playerid, vehicleid)
{
PlayerPlaySound(playerid, 12201, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
return 1;
}

if(newstate == 2)
{
TextDrawShowForPlayer(playerid, Speedometr[playerid][0]);
TextDrawShowForPlayer(playerid, Speedometr[playerid][1]);
TextDrawShowForPlayer(playerid, Speedometr[playerid][2]);
}
else
{
TextDrawHideForPlayer(playerid, Speedometr[playerid][0]);
TextDrawHideForPlayer(playerid, Speedometr[playerid][1]);
TextDrawHideForPlayer(playerid, Speedometr[playerid][2]);
}
if(Death[playerid] == 1){RemovePlayerFromVehicle(playerid);}
return 1;
}

}

{

{

}

{

return 1;

public OnRconLoginAttempt(ip[], password[], success)
{
if(!success)
{
new YouIP[16];
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
{
GetPlayerIp(i, YouIP, sizeof(YouIP));
if(!strcmp(ip, YouIP, true))
{
new str[256];
PlayerPlaySound(i, 42801, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
format(str,sizeof str,"~r~увага !!!~n~~r~за таку фiгню~n~~y~IP ~g~%s ~n~~y~може бути ~r~забанений...",ip);
GameTextForPlayer(i, str , 45000, 3);
ClearChat(i, 0);
SetTimerEx("PlayKick", 5000, 0, "i", i);
return 1;
}
}
}
}
return 1;
}

public OnPlayerUpdate(playerid)
{
if(GetPlayerState(playerid) == 2)
{
SetSpeedometrDel(playerid);
SetSpeedometrPok(playerid);
}

if( GetPlayerMoney ( playerid ) != GGetPlayerMoney ( playerid ) ) ResetPlayerMoney( playerid ), GivePlayerMoney( playerid, GGetPlayerMoney ( playerid ) );
NETafkPl[playerid][0] = 0;
new Float:deathcrack;
GetPlayerHealth(playerid,deathcrack);
if (deathcrack < 15.0){
Death[playerid] = 1;
DeathAnimation(playerid,"CRACK","crckdeth2", 4.0, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0);
return 1;
}
if (deathcrack > 15.0 && Death[playerid] == 1){
Death[playerid] = 0;
ClearAnimations(playerid);
return 1;
}
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig1] == 0)
{
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig1] == 1) return 1;
if (PlayerInfo[playerid][pKills] >= 100) SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, ""), PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig1] = 1, SetPVarInt(playerid, "PlMon", GetPVarInt(playerid, "PlMon") + 0);
}
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig2] == 0)
{
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig2] == 1) return 1;
if (PlayerInfo[playerid][pKills] >= 1000) SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, ""), PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig2] = 1, SetPVarInt(playerid, "PlMon", GetPVarInt(playerid, "PlMon") + 0);
}
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig3] == 0)
{
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig3] == 1) return 1;
if (PlayerInfo[playerid][pKills] >= 3000) SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, ""), PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig3] = 1, SetPVarInt(playerid, "PlMon", GetPVarInt(playerid, "PlMon") + 0);
}
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig4] == 0)
{
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig4] == 1) return 1;
if (GangLvl[playerid] == 6) SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, ""), PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig4] = 1,	SetPVarInt(playerid, "PlMon", GetPVarInt(playerid, "PlMon") + 0);
}
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig5] == 0)
{
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig5] == 1) return 1;
if (PlayerInfo[playerid][pAdmin] >= 1) SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, ""), PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig5] = 1,	SetPVarInt(playerid, "PlMon", GetPVarInt(playerid, "PlMon") + 0);
}
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig6] == 0)
{
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig6] == 1) return 1;
if (PlayerInfo[playerid][pAdmin] >= 3) SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, ""), PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig6] = 1,	SetPVarInt(playerid, "PlMon", GetPVarInt(playerid, "PlMon") + 0);
}
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig7] == 0)
{
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig7] == 1) return 1;
if(GGetPlayerMoney(playerid) >= 100000000) SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, ""), PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig7] = 1,	SetPVarInt(playerid, "PlMon", GetPVarInt(playerid, "PlMon") + 0);
}
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig8] == 0)
{
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig8] == 1) return 1;
if (PlayerInfo[playerid][pAdmin] >= 7) SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, ""), PlayerInfo[playerid][pDostig8] = 1,	SetPVarInt(playerid, "PlMon", GetPVarInt(playerid, "PlMon") + 0);
}
return 1;
}

{

{

{
new day,yy,mm,dd,ip[256];

GetPlayerIp(player[playerid],ip,sizeof(ip));
for(new Index = strlen(inputtext)-1; Index != -1; Index--)
switch(inputtext[Index])
{
case '0'..'9': continue;
default: return SendClientMessage(playerid,0xFF0606AA,"BOBBBO SERVER : {FFFF00}Днi бану повиннi бути вiд 1/до 15 !");
}
if(day <= 0)

return 1;
}
if(day > 15)
{

format(string, sizeof(string), "{00FFFF}Обрано IP : {FF00FF}%s\n{00FFFF}Введiть кiлькiсть днiв бану IP гравця:\nГравець: {FFFF00}%s [%d]", ip, RealName[player[playerid]], player[playerid]);

SendClientMessageToAll(0xF8825AAA,string);

getdate(timedata[2], timedata[3], timedata[4]);
dd = timedata[4];
mm = timedata[3];
yy = timedata[2];
if((timedata[2] - 8)%4 == 0)
{//високосний
if(timedata[3] == 1 || timedata[3] == 3 || timedata[3] == 5 || timedata[3] == 7 || timedata[3] == 9 || timedata[3] == 11)
{
dd = day+timedata[4];
if(day+timedata[4] > 31)
{
mm++;
dd = (day+timedata[4])-31;
if(timedata[3] > 12)
{
mm=mm-12;
yy++;
}
}
}
if(timedata[3] == 4 || timedata[3] == 6 || timedata[3] == 8 || timedata[3] == 10 || timedata[3] == 12)
{
dd = day+timedata[4];
if(day+timedata[4] > 30)
{
mm++;
dd = (day+timedata[4])-30;
if(timedata[3] > 12)
{
mm=mm-12;
yy++;
}
}
}
if(timedata[3] == 2)
{
dd = day+timedata[4];
if(day+timedata[4] > 29)
{
mm++;
dd = (day+timedata[4])-29;
if(timedata[3] > 12)
{
mm=mm-12;
yy++;
}
}
}
}
else
{//не високосний
if(timedata[3] == 1 || timedata[3] == 3 || timedata[3] == 5 || timedata[3] == 7 || timedata[3] == 9 || timedata[3] == 11)
{
dd = day+timedata[4];
if(day+timedata[4] > 31)
{
mm++;
dd = (day+timedata[4])-31;
if(timedata[3] > 12)
{
mm=mm-12;
yy++;
}
}
}

{
dd = day+timedata[4];
if(day+timedata[4] > 30)
{
mm++;
dd = (day+timedata[4])-30;
if(timedata[3] > 12)
{
mm=mm-12;
yy++;
}
}
}
if(timedata[3] == 2)
{
dd = day+timedata[4];
if(day+timedata[4] > 28)
{
mm++;
dd = (day+timedata[4])-28;
if(timedata[3] > 12)
{
mm=mm-12;
yy++;
}
}
}

forward DelAkk22(para1);
public DelAkk22(para1)
{

new para3[130];
strdel(para3, 0, 130);
strcat(para3, GName[para1]);

strdel(GHead[para1], 0, 64);
strdel(GName[para1], 0, 130);
strdel(GColor[para1], 0, 16);
strdel(GColorHex[para1], 0, 16);
GSpawnX[para1] = 0.00;
GSpawnY[para1] = 0.00;
GSpawnZ[para1] = 0.00;
GInter[para1] = 0;
GWorld[para1] = 0;
GSkin[para1][0] = 500;
GSkin[para1][1] = 500;
GSkin[para1][2] = 500;
GSkin[para1][3] = 500;
GSkin[para1][4] = 500;
GSkin[para1][5] = 500;
GPlayers[para1] = 0;
fremove(string);
format(ssss,sizeof(ssss)," *** i видалив банду [%s{33CCFF}] (автоматично) .", para3);
SendClientMessageToAll(0x33CCFFFF, ssss);
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
{
if(PGang[i] == para1)
{
SendClientMessage(i, 0xFF0000FF, "Ваша банда була видалена !");
PGang[i] = 0;
GangLvl[i] = 0;
}
}
}
SetTimerEx("DelAkk33", 300, 0, "i", para1);
return 1;
}

forward GangLoad();
public GangLoad()
{
new file, f[256];
for(new i=1; i<(MAX_GANGS - 1); i++)
{
format(f, 256, "gangs/%i.ini", i);
file = ini_openFile(f);
if(file == INI_OK)
{
ini_getString(file, "Gang TDReg", GTDReg[i]);
ini_getString(file, "Gang head", GHead[i]);
ini_getString(file, "Gang name", GName[i]);
ini_getString(file, "Gang color", GColor[i]);
ini_getFloat(file, "SpawnX", GSpawnX[i]);
ini_getFloat(file, "SpawnY", GSpawnY[i]);
ini_getFloat(file, "SpawnZ", GSpawnZ[i]);
ini_getInteger(file, "GInter", GInter[i]);
ini_getInteger(file, "GWorld", GWorld[i]);
ini_getInteger(file, "Skin1", GSkin[i][0]);
ini_getInteger(file, "Skin2", GSkin[i][1]);
ini_getInteger(file, "Skin3", GSkin[i][2]);
ini_getInteger(file, "Skin4", GSkin[i][3]);
ini_getInteger(file, "Skin5", GSkin[i][4]);
ini_getInteger(file, "Skin6", GSkin[i][5]);
ini_getInteger(file, "Players", GPlayers[i]);
ini_closeFile(file);
Gang[i] = 1;
GangSA[i] = 1;
}
else
{
Gang[i] = 0;
GangSA[i] = 0;
}
GColorDec[i] = HexToInt(GColor[i]);
strdel(GColorHex[i], 0, 16);
strcat(GColorHex[i], ColorRes(GColor[i]));
}
return true;
}

public GangSave(gangid)
{
if(GangSA[gangid] == 1)
{

if(file == INI_OK)
{

ini_setString(file, "Gang head", GHead[gangid]);

ini_setString(file, "Gang color", GColor[gangid]);

ini_setFloat(file, "SpawnZ", GSpawnZ[gangid]);
ini_setInteger(file, "GInter", GInter[gangid]);
ini_setInteger(file, "GWorld", GWorld[gangid]);
ini_setInteger(file, "Skin1", GSkin[gangid][0]);
ini_setInteger(file, "Skin2", GSkin[gangid][1]);
ini_setInteger(file, "Skin3", GSkin[gangid][2]);
ini_setInteger(file, "Skin4", GSkin[gangid][3]);
ini_setInteger(file, "Skin5", GSkin[gangid][4]);

stock HexToInt(string[])
{
if(string[0] == 0) { return 0; }
new i;
new cur=1;
new res=0;
for(i = strlen(string); i > 0; i--)
{
if(string[i-1] < 58)
{
res = res  +cur * (string[i-1] - 48);
}
else
{
res = res + cur * (string[i-1] - 65 + 10);
}
cur = cur * 16;
}
return res;
}

stock ColorRes(string[])
{
new string555[16];
strmid(string555, string, 0, 6, sizeof(string555));
new dop11;
dop11 = HexToInt(string555);
new dopper[7];
dopper[0] = 48;
new dop22 = 0;
if(dop11 > 16777215)
{
dop22 = dop11 / 16777216;
dop11 = dop11 - (dop22 * 16777216);
if(dop22 > 9)
{
dopper[0] = dop22 + 55;
}
else
{
dopper[0] = dop22 + 48;
}
}
new dop33 = 1048576;
for(new j = 1; j < 7; j++)
{
dop22 = dop11 / dop33;
dop11 = dop11 - (dop22 * dop33);
if(dop22 > 9)
{
dopper[j] = dop22 + 55;
}
else
{
dopper[j] = dop22 + 48;
}
dop33 = dop33 / 16;
}
strdel(string555, 0, 16);
strmid(string555, dopper, 1, 7, sizeof(string555));
return string555;
}

forward DestrCar(playerid);
public DestrCar(playerid)
{
if(GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid) != 0)
{
new Float:igx, Float:igy, Float:igz;
GetPlayerPos(playerid, igx, igy, igz);
SetPlayerPos(playerid, igx+3, igy+3, igz+5);
}
if(playcar[playerid] != 0)
{
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
if(playcar[playerid] == neon[i][2])
{
DestroyObject(neon[i][0]);
DestroyObject(neon[i][1]);
neon[i][0] = 0;
neon[i][1] = 0;
neon[i][2] = 0;
}
}
if(neon[playerid][0] != 0) { DestroyObject(neon[playerid][0]); }
if(neon[playerid][1] != 0) { DestroyObject(neon[playerid][1]); }
neon[playerid][0] = 0;
neon[playerid][1] = 0;
neon[playerid][2] = 0;
DestroyVehicle(playcar[playerid]);
playcar[playerid] = 0;
}
return 1;
}

forward LogTelPort(playerid, regm, per1, per2, Float:per3, Float:cor1, Float:cor2, Float:cor3);
public LogTelPort(playerid, regm, per1, per2, Float:per3, Float:cor1, Float:cor2, Float:cor3)
{
new carpl, modelcar;
carpl = GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid);
modelcar = GetVehicleModel(carpl);
if(modelcar != 432)
{
SetTimerEx("TelPort", 300, 0, "ddddffff", playerid, regm, per1, per2, Float:per3, Float:cor1, Float:cor2 ,Float:cor3);
}
else
{
SetTimerEx("TelPort", 300, 0, "ddddffff", playerid, regm, per1, per2, Float:per3, Float:cor1, Float:cor2, Float:cor3);
TelPortDop11(playerid, regm, per1, per2, Float:per3, Float:cor1, Float:cor2, Float:cor3);
TelPortDop22(playerid, regm, per1, per2, Float:per3, Float:cor1 ,Float:cor2, Float:cor3);
}
return 1;
}

forward TelPort(playerid, regm, per1, per2, Float:per3, Float:cor1, Float:cor2, Float:cor3);
public TelPort(playerid, regm, per1, per2, Float:per3, Float:cor1, Float:cor2, Float:cor3)
{
if(regm == 0)
{
new car;
new Float:angle;
car = GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid);
GetVehicleZAngle(car, angle);
SetVehicleZAngle(car, angle);
return 1;
}
if(regm == 1)
{
SetPlayerInterior(playerid, per1);
SetPlayerVirtualWorld(playerid, per2);
new VID = GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid);
new Float:angle;
LinkVehicleToInterior(VID, per1);
SetVehicleVirtualWorld(VID, per2);
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
{
if(GetPlayerVehicleID(i) == VID && i != playerid)
{
SetPlayerInterior(i, per1);
SetPlayerVirtualWorld(i, per2);
}
}
}
SetVehiclePos(VID, cor1, cor2, cor3);
GetVehicleZAngle(VID, angle);
SetVehicleZAngle(VID, angle);
SetPlayerPos(playerid, cor1, cor2, cor3);
PutPlayerInVehicle(playerid, VID, 0);
return 1;
}
if(regm == 2)
{
SetPlayerInterior(playerid, per1);
SetPlayerVirtualWorld(playerid, per2);
new VID = GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid);
LinkVehicleToInterior(VID, per1);
SetVehicleVirtualWorld(VID, per2);
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
{
if(GetPlayerVehicleID(i) == VID && i != playerid)
{
SetPlayerInterior(i, per1);
SetPlayerVirtualWorld(i, per2);
}
}
}
SetVehiclePos(VID, cor1, cor2, cor3);
SetVehicleZAngle(VID, per3);
SetPlayerPos(playerid, cor1, cor2, cor3);
PutPlayerInVehicle(playerid, VID, 0);
}
return 1;
}

forward entcar22(playerid, testcar);
public entcar22(playerid, testcar)
{
new dopper = -600;
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
{
if(GetPlayerVehicleID(i) == testcar && GetPlayerVehicleSeat(i) == 0)
{
dopper = i;
}
}
}
if(dopper != -600)
{
new Float:x, Float:y, Float:z;
GetPlayerPos(dopper, x, y, z);
SetPlayerPos(dopper, x+3, y+3, z);
new string[256];
format(string, sizeof(string), " *** Адмiн %s висадив гравця %s [%d] з транспорту  ID: %d  по командi /entercar",
RealName[playerid], RealName[dopper], dopper, testcar);
SendAdminMessage(0xFFFF00FF, string);
}
SetPlayerVirtualWorld(playerid, GetVehicleVirtualWorld(testcar));
SetTimerEx("entcar33", 300, 0, "ii", playerid, testcar);
return 1;
}

forward RestartS();
public RestartS()
{
restrest = 1;
new per;
SendClientMessageToAll(0xFF0000FF,"***РЕСТАРТ***");
SendRconCommand("reloadlog");
printf("================================ РЕСТАРТ СЕРВЕРА: ==================================");
KillTimer(fivesectimer);
KillTimer(restart);
KillTimer(autorepaircar);
KillTimer(onsectimer);
KillTimer(minsertimer);
KillTimer(timer200);
KillTimer(timpolsec);
KillTimer(ServerTimerOne);
KillTimer(ServerTimerTwo);

SetTimerEx("ResServ", 1000, 0, "i", per);
return 1;
}

forward ResServ(per);
public ResServ(per)
{
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
TextDrawHideForPlayer(i, TScore[i]);
TextDrawDestroy(TScore[i]);
if(mapiconid[i] != -600)
{
DestroyDynamicMapIcon(mapiconid[i]);
}
mapiconid[i] = -600;
if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
{
PlayKick(i);
}
}
SetTimerEx("ResServ222", 5000, 0, "i", per);
return 1;
}

forward PassControl(string[]);
public PassControl(string[])
{
new dln, dopper;
dln = strlen(string);
dopper = 1;
for(new i = 0; i < dln; i++)
{
if(string[i] < 48 || (string[i] > 57 && string[i] < 65) ||
(string[i] > 90 && string[i] < 97) || string[i] > 122) { dopper = 0; }
}
return dopper;
}
forward InpTxtControl(string[]);
public InpTxtControl(string[])
{
new dln, dopper;
dln = strlen(string);
dopper = 1;
for(new i = 0; i < dln; i++)
{
if(string[i] < 32 || string[i] == 37 || string[i] == 126 ||
string[i] == 127 || string[i] == 152 || string[i] == 160) { dopper = 0; }
}
return dopper;
}
forward VehicSpawn(playerid, vehid, vehcol1, vehcol2, dispz);
public VehicSpawn(playerid, vehid, vehcol1, vehcol2, dispz)
{
if(GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid) == playcar[playerid] && playcar[playerid] != 0)
{
new Float:igx, Float:igy, Float:igz;
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
{
if(GetPlayerVehicleID(i) == playcar[playerid] && playerid != i)
{
GetPlayerPos(i, igx, igy, igz);
SetPlayerPos(i, igx+3, igy+3, igz);
}
if(admper1[i] != 600 && admper1[i] == playerid)
{
admper5[i] = 2;
}
}
}
}
if(GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid) != playcar[playerid] && IsPlayerInAnyVehicle(playerid))
{
new Float:igx, Float:igy, Float:igz;
GetPlayerPos(playerid, igx, igy, igz);
SetPlayerPos(playerid, igx+3, igy+3, igz);
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
{
if(admper1[i] != 600 && admper1[i] == playerid)
{
admper5[i] = 2;
}
}
}
}
SetTimerEx("VehicSecSpawn", 300, 0, "iiiii", playerid, vehid, vehcol1, vehcol2, dispz);
return 1;
}
forward VehicSecSpawn(playerid, vehid, vehcol1, vehcol2, dispz);
public VehicSecSpawn(playerid, vehid, vehcol1, vehcol2, dispz)
{
new Float:x, Float:y, Float:z, Float:Angle;
GetPlayerPos(playerid, x, y, z);
if (GetPlayerState(playerid) == 2 || GetPlayerState(playerid) == 3)
{
GetVehicleZAngle(GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid), Angle);
}
else
{
GetPlayerFacingAngle(playerid, Angle);
}
new plvw;
plvw = GetPlayerVirtualWorld(playerid);
if(playcar[playerid] == 0)
{
playcar[playerid] = CreateVehicle(vehid, x, y, z+dispz, Angle, vehcol1, vehcol2, 90000);
LinkVehicleToInterior(playcar[playerid], GetPlayerInterior(playerid));
SetVehicleVirtualWorld(playcar[playerid], plvw);
PutPlayerInVehicle(playerid, playcar[playerid], 0);
}else{
if(playcar[playerid] == neon[playerid][2])
{
DestroyVehicle(playcar[playerid]);
playcar[playerid] = CreateVehicle(vehid, x, y, z+dispz, Angle, vehcol1, vehcol2, 90000);
LinkVehicleToInterior(playcar[playerid], GetPlayerInterior(playerid));
SetVehicleVirtualWorld(playcar[playerid], plvw);
PutPlayerInVehicle(playerid, playcar[playerid], 0);
AttachObjectToVehicle(neon[playerid][0], playcar[playerid], -0.8, 0.0, -0.70, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
AttachObjectToVehicle(neon[playerid][1], playcar[playerid], 0.8, 0.0, -0.70, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
neon[playerid][2] = playcar[playerid];
}
else
{
new dopper = 0;
new dopper22 = -600;
while(dopper < MAX_PLAYERS)
{
if(playcar[playerid] == neon[dopper][2] && playerid != dopper)
{
dopper22 = dopper;
break;
}
dopper++;
}
if(dopper22 != -600)
{
DestroyVehicle(playcar[playerid]);
playcar[playerid] = CreateVehicle(vehid, x, y, z+dispz, Angle, vehcol1, vehcol2, 90000);
LinkVehicleToInterior(playcar[playerid], GetPlayerInterior(playerid));
SetVehicleVirtualWorld(playcar[playerid], plvw);
PutPlayerInVehicle(playerid, playcar[playerid], 0);
AttachObjectToVehicle(neon[dopper22][0], playcar[playerid], -0.8, 0.0, -0.70, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
AttachObjectToVehicle(neon[dopper22][1], playcar[playerid], 0.8, 0.0, -0.70, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
neon[dopper22][2] = playcar[playerid];
}
else
{
DestroyVehicle(playcar[playerid]);
playcar[playerid] = CreateVehicle(vehid, x, y, z+dispz, Angle, vehcol1, vehcol2, 90000);
LinkVehicleToInterior(playcar[playerid], GetPlayerInterior(playerid));
SetVehicleVirtualWorld(playcar[playerid], plvw);
PutPlayerInVehicle(playerid, playcar[playerid], 0);
}
}
}
return 1;
}
forward DubTlp(playerid);
public DubTlp(playerid)
{
if(GetPlayerState(playerid) == 2)
{
new regm = 2, per1, per2, Float:per3;
per1 = TpPosP[playerid][0];
per2 = TpPosP[playerid][1];
per3 = TpDestP[playerid][3];
LogTelPort(playerid, regm, per1, per2, Float:per3, Float:TpDestP[playerid][0], Float:TpDestP[playerid][1],
Float:TpDestP[playerid][2]+1);
}
else
{
SetPlayerInterior(playerid, TpPosP[playerid][0]);
SetPlayerVirtualWorld(playerid, TpPosP[playerid][1]);
SetPlayerPos(playerid, TpDestP[playerid][0], TpDestP[playerid][1], TpDestP[playerid][2]+1);
SetPlayerFacingAngle(playerid, TpDestP[playerid][3]);
SetCameraBehindPlayer(playerid);
}
SendClientMessage(playerid, 0x00FF00FF, " Ви були телепортованi на збережену позицiю.");
return 1;
}

scou++;
}
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pAdmin] >= 1 && PlayerInfo[i][pAdmin] == 2 && PlayerInfo[i][pAdmshad] == 1)
{
format(string, sizeof(string), " [%d]", i);
strins(NamAdm[scou], string, 0, 64);
strins(NamAdm[scou], RealName[i], 0, 64);
strins(NamAdm[scou], "2 LVL: ", 0, 64);
strins(NamAdm[scou], "(s) ", 0, 64);
scou++;
}
}
}
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
{
if(PlayerInfo[i][pAdmin] == 1 && PlayerInfo[i][pAdmshad] == 0)
{
format(string, sizeof(string), " [%d]", i);
strins(NamAdm[scou], string, 0, 64);
strins(NamAdm[scou], RealName[i], 0, 64);
strins(NamAdm[scou], "1 LVL: ", 0, 64);
strins(NamAdm[scou], "     ", 0, 64);
scou++;
}
if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pAdmin] >= 1 && PlayerInfo[i][pAdmin] == 1 && PlayerInfo[i][pAdmshad] == 1)
{
format(string, sizeof(string), " [%d]", i);
strins(NamAdm[scou], string, 0, 64);
strins(NamAdm[scou], RealName[i], 0, 64);
strins(NamAdm[scou], "1 LVL: ", 0, 64);
strins(NamAdm[scou], "(s) ", 0, 64);
scou++;
}
}
}
format(string,sizeof(string),"%s\n%s\n%s\n%s\n%s\n%s\n%s\n%s\n%s\n%s\n%s\n%s\n%s\n%s\n%s\n%s\n%s\n%s\n%s\n%s",

ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, 2, 0, "{00FF00}            Адмiни онлайн:", string, "{00FF00}OK", "");

}
return 1;
}

forward RepairCar();
public RepairCar()
{
new swper, locmoney, locmoney22, locscore, locscore22;
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
{
if(autorepair[i] == 1 && GetPlayerState(i) == 2)
{
new car = GetPlayerVehicleID(i);
RepairVehicle(car);
SetVehicleHealth(car, 1000);
}
swper = 0;
if(NETafkPl[i][0] > 5) {NETafkPl[i][0] = 5;}
if(NETafkPl[i][0] < 5 && NETafkPl[i][3] == 5)
{
NETafkPl[i][4] = 1;
}
else
{
NETafkPl[i][4] = 0;
}
NETafkPl[i][3] = NETafkPl[i][0];
if(NETafkPl[i][0] == 5)
{
NETafkPl[i][5] = 1;
if(PlayerInfo[i][pAdmin] == 0)
{
NETafkPl[i][1]++;
}
NETafkPl[i][2] = 0;
if(NETafkPl[i][1] >= 150)
{
NETafkPl[i][1] = 0;
PlayerInfo[i][pMinlog] = PlayerInfo[i][pMinlog] - 4;
swper = 1;
}
}
if(NETafkPl[i][0] < 5)
{
NETafkPl[i][5] = 0;
if(NETafkPl[i][2] <= 3 && NETafkPl[i][1] > 0)
{
NETafkPl[i][2]++;
if(PlayerInfo[i][pAdmin] == 0)
{
NETafkPl[i][1]++;
}
}
else
{
NETafkPl[i][1] = 0;
NETafkPl[i][2] = 0;
}
}
if(gPlayerLogged[i] == 1)
{
locmoney = GGetPlayerMoney(i);
locscore = GetPlayerScore(i);
if(GetPVarInt(i, "MonControl") == 2)
{
moneycontrol[i] = locmoney;
SetPVarInt(i, "MonControl", 0);
}
if(GetPVarInt(i, "MonControl") == 1)
{
SetPVarInt(i, "MonControl", 2);
}
if(GetPVarInt(i, "MonControl") == 0)
{
locmoney22 = locmoney - moneycontrol[i];
if(locmoney22 > 10000 || locmoney22 < -1000000)
{
swper = 2;
moneycontrol22[i] = 1;
}
}
if(GetPVarInt(i, "ScorControl") == 2)
{
scorecontrol[i] = locscore;
SetPVarInt(i, "ScorControl", 0);
}
if(GetPVarInt(i, "ScorControl") == 1)
{
SetPVarInt(i, "ScorControl", 2);
}
if(GetPVarInt(i, "ScorControl") == 0)
{
locscore22 = locscore - scorecontrol[i];
if(locscore22 > 10 || locscore22 < -100)
{
swper = 3;
scorecontrol22[i] = 1;
}
}
if(swper != 0)
{
new string[256];
switch(swper)
{
case 1: format(string, sizeof(string), "* Гравець {FFFF00}%s [%d] {FF0000}був кiкнутий - щось затримався в AFK !", RealName[i], i);
case 2: format(string, sizeof(string), "* Гравець {FFFF00}%s [%d] {FF0000}був кiкнутий - пiдозра на накрутку грошей !", RealName[i], i);
case 3: format(string, sizeof(string), "* Гравець {FFFF00}%s [%d] {FF0000}був кiкнутий - пiдозра на накрутку очок  !", RealName[i], i);
}
SendClientMessageToAll(0xFF0000FF, string);
SetTimerEx("PlayKick", 300, 0, "i", i);
}
}
}
}
return 1;
}

forward Timer200ms();
public Timer200ms()
{
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++){
if(IsPlayerConnected(i)){
NETafkPl[i][0]++;
SetPVarInt(i, "AdmLvl", PlayerInfo[i][pAdmin]);
SetPVarInt(i, "PlGng", PGang[i]);
SetPVarInt(i, "PlGLvl", GangLvl[i]);
if(PlayerInfo[i][pAdmlive] == 1){
SetPlayerHealth(i, 10200);
SetPlayerArmour(i, 10200);
livdop[i] = 1;}
if(PlayerInfo[i][pAdmlive] == 0 && livdop[i] == 1){
SetPlayerHealth(i, 100);
SetPlayerArmour(i, 100);
livdop[i] = 0;}}}
return 1;
}

forward PolSec();
public PolSec()
{

for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++){
if(IsPlayerConnected(i)){
if(playspa[i] == 1){


if(Glow[i]==1){
GlowColor = GlowColor+1;
if(GlowColor==9){
GlowColor=0;
}
SetPlayerColor(i,GlowColors[GlowColor]);
}

}
if(PlayLock1[0][i] != 600 && playspa[i] == 1){
SetPlayerInterior(i, PlayLock1[1][i]);
SetPlayerVirtualWorld(i, PlayLock1[2][i]);
SetPlayerPos(i, PlayLock2[0][i], PlayLock2[1][i], PlayLock2[2][i]);
SetPlayerFacingAngle(i, PlayLock2[3][i]);
SetCameraBehindPlayer(i);}}}
return 1;
}
forward OneSecOnd();
public OneSecOnd()
{
new PlayVeh;
new swper;
new play333weap[13], play333ammo[13], dopper333;
new Float:PosX, Float:PosY, Float:PosZ;
new playnam333[MAX_PLAYER_NAME];
new string[256];

if(nucexplos == 1)
{
SetWeather(19);
SetWorldTime(0);
}
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
{
if(nucexplos == 1)//если на сервере ядерный взрыв, то:
{
if(SnowONOFF[i] == 1)
{
new Float:hp;
SetPlayerArmour(i, 0);
GetPlayerHealth(i, hp);
SetPlayerHealth(i, hp-10);
GetPlayerCameraPos(i, PosX, PosY, PosZ);
MovePlayerObject(i, snowobj[i], PosX, PosY, PosZ-5, 9999.0);
}
}
PlayVeh = GetPlayerVehicleID(admper1[i]);
if(admper1[i] != 600)
{
if(PlayVeh != 0 && admper5[i] == 0)
{
PlayerSpectateVehicle(i, PlayVeh, SPECTATE_MODE_NORMAL);
admper5[i] = 1;
}
if(PlayVeh == 0 && admper5[i] == 1)
{
PlayerSpectatePlayer(i, admper1[i], SPECTATE_MODE_NORMAL);
admper5[i] = 0;
}
if(admper5[i] == 3)
{
PlayerSpectateVehicle(i, PlayVeh, SPECTATE_MODE_NORMAL);
admper5[i] = 1;
}
if(admper5[i] == 2)
{
PlayerSpectatePlayer(i, admper1[i], SPECTATE_MODE_NORMAL);
admper5[i] = 3;
}
if(admper6[i] == 2)
{
admper6[i] = 0;
}
if(admper6[i] == 1)
{
SetPlayerInterior(i, GetPlayerInterior(admper1[i]));
SetPlayerVirtualWorld(i, GetPlayerVirtualWorld(admper1[i]));
if(PlayVeh != 0)
{
PlayerSpectateVehicle(i, PlayVeh, SPECTATE_MODE_NORMAL);
admper5[i] = 1;
}
else
{
PlayerSpectatePlayer(i, admper1[i], SPECTATE_MODE_NORMAL);
admper5[i] = 0;
}
admper6[i] = 2;
}
if(((GetPlayerInterior(i) != GetPlayerInterior(admper1[i])) ||
(GetPlayerVirtualWorld(i) != GetPlayerVirtualWorld(admper1[i]))) && admper6[i] == 0)
{
admper6[i] = 1;
}
}
if(PlayerInfo[i][pMutedsec] > 0)
{
PlayerInfo[i][pMutedsec]--;
if(PlayerInfo[i][pMutedsec] <= 0)
{
PlayerInfo[i][pMutedsec] = 0;
format(string, sizeof(string), "* Гравець %s [%d] розiткнутий.", RealName[i], i);
SendClientMessageToAll(0x00FF00FF, string);
}
}
if(PlayerInfo[i][pPrisonsec] > 0)
{
if(playspa[i] == 1)
{
PlayerInfo[i][pPrisonsec]--;
format(string, sizeof(string), "~n~~n~~n~~n~~n~~n~~n~~g~Вам залишилось сидiти:~n~~r~%d",PlayerInfo[i][pPrisonsec]);
GameTextForPlayer(i, string, 1500, 3);
}
if(PlayerInfo[i][pPrisonsec] <= 0)
{
PlayerInfo[i][pPrisonsec] = 0;
format(string, sizeof(string), "* Гравець %s [%d] звiльнений з пiд арешту.", RealName[i], i);
SendClientMessageToAll(0x00FF00FF, string);
weapstatplay[i] = 0;
OnPlayerSpawn(i);
//StopAudioStreamForPlayer(i);
//PlayAudioStreamForPlayer(i, "http://online.radiorelax.ua/RadioRelax_Cafe");// вихід з тюрми
//PlayAudioStreamForPlayer(i, "OFF");
}
}

if(countdown[i]>0)
{
countdown[i]-=1;
new str[16];
format(str,16,"~r~- ~g~%d ~r~-",countdown[i]);
GameTextForPlayer(i,str,940,3);
PlayerPlaySound(i,41603,0.0,0.0,0.0);
if(countdown[i]<4)TogglePlayerControllable(i,0);
}
if(countdown[i]==0)
{
TogglePlayerControllable(i,1);
GameTextForPlayer(i,"~g~П О Г Н А Л И !!!~n~~y~П О Г Н А Л И !!!~n~~r~П О Г Н А Л И !!!",1800,3);
StopAudioStreamForPlayer(i);
PlayAudioStreamForPlayer(i, "http://is.gd/forsazh_3");// старт!!!
PlayerPlaySound(i,3200,0.0,0.0,0.0);
countdown[i]=-1;
}


swper = 0;
if(playspa[i] == 0)
{
oneminkick[i]++;
if(oneminkick[i] >= 180)
{
swper = 1;
oneminkick[i] = 0;
}
}
else
{
oneminkick[i] = 0;
}
GetPlayerName(i, playnam333, sizeof(playnam333));
if(strcmp(playnam333, RealName[i], false) != 0)
{
swper = 2;
}
GetPlayerPos(i, PosX, PosY, PosZ);
if(playspa[i] == 1 && PlayerInfo[i][pPrisonsec] > 0)
{
if(prisoncount[i] == 3)
{
if(PosX < 213 || PosX > 231 || PosY < 107 || PosY > 127 || PosZ < 997 || PosZ > 1003)
{
SetPVarInt(i, "ScorControl", 3);
SetPlayerScore(i,GetPlayerScore(i)-50);

forward FiveSecTimer();
public FiveSecTimer()
{

{
if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
{
if(playspa[i] == 1)
{
if(SnowONOFF[i] == 1)
{
SendClientMessage(i, 0xFF0000FF, " УВАГА !!! На серверi був зпричинений ЯДЕРНИЙ ВИБУХ !!!");
SendClientMessage(i, 0xFF0000FF, " Радiацiйний фон превищено в тисячi разiв !!! Рятуйтесь хто як може.....");
SendClientMessage(i, 0xFF0000FF, " НЕБЕЗПЕКА!!!DANGER!!!НЕБЕЗПЕКА!!!DANGER!!!НЕБЕЗПЕКА!!!");
}
format(string, sizeof(string), "%08d", GetPlayerScore(i));
TextDrawSetString(TScore[i], string);
TextDrawShowForPlayer(i, TScore[i]);
if(GetPlayerScore(i) < 0)
{
TextDrawColor(TScore[i], 0xFF0000FF);
}
else
{
TextDrawColor(TScore[i], 0xFFA500FF);
}
if(GangLvl[i] == 6){SetPlayerWantedLevel(i, 6);}
if(GangLvl[i] == 5){SetPlayerWantedLevel(i, 5);}
if(GangLvl[i] == 4){SetPlayerWantedLevel(i, 4);}
if(GangLvl[i] == 3){SetPlayerWantedLevel(i, 3);}
if(GangLvl[i] == 2){SetPlayerWantedLevel(i, 2);}
if(GangLvl[i] == 1){SetPlayerWantedLevel(i, 1);}
if(GangLvl[i] <= 0){SetPlayerWantedLevel(i, 0);}
}
}
}
return 1;
}
forward PlayerUpdate();
public PlayerUpdate()
{
for(new Player; Player < GetMaxPlayers(); Player++)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(Player) && GetPlayerState(Player) == PLAYER_STATE_DRIVER && VehicleIsCar(GetPlayerVehicleID(Player))) GetVehiclePos(GetPlayerVehicleID(Player),PlayerPositionX[Player],PlayerPositionY[Player],PlayerPositionZ[Player]);

}
return 1;
}
forward PlayerDrift();
public PlayerDrift()
{
for(new Player; Player < GetMaxPlayers(); Player++)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(Player) && GetPlayerState(Player) == PLAYER_STATE_DRIVER && VehicleIsCar(GetPlayerVehicleID(Player)))
{
new Float:Angle;
GetVehicleZAngle(GetPlayerVehicleID(Player),Angle);
if(floatabs(floatsub(Angle,PlayerTheoreticAngle(Player))) < 80.0 && floatabs(floatsub(Angle,PlayerTheoreticAngle(Player))) > 33.0 && VehicleSpeed(GetPlayerVehicleID(Player)) < 166 && VehicleSpeed(GetPlayerVehicleID(Player)) > 27)
{
if(PlayerMoney[Player] == 0 && PlayerScore[Player] == 0 && PlayerCombo[Player] == 1)
{
TextDrawShowForPlayer(Player,ServerTextDrawThree[Player]);
TextDrawShowForPlayer(Player,ServerTextDrawFour[Player]);
TextDrawShowForPlayer(Player,ServerTextDrawFive[Player]);
TextDrawSetString(ServerTextDrawThree[Player]," ");
TextDrawSetString(ServerTextDrawFour[Player]," ");
TextDrawSetString(ServerTextDrawFive[Player]," ");
}
PlayerMoney[Player] += floatround(floatabs(floatsub(Angle,PlayerTheoreticAngle(Player))) * (VehicleSpeed(GetPlayerVehicleID(Player)) * 0.1))/70;
PlayerScore[Player] = (PlayerMoney[Player] += floatround(floatabs(floatsub(Angle,PlayerTheoreticAngle(Player))) * (VehicleSpeed(GetPlayerVehicleID(Player)) * 0.1))/70)/300;
PlayerCombo[Player] = PlayerScore[Player] / 3;
if(PlayerCombo[Player] < 1) PlayerCombo[Player] = 1;
new String[128];
format(String,sizeof(String),"дрифт  ~g~~H~$ %d",PlayerMoney[Player]);
TextDrawSetString(ServerTextDrawThree[Player],String);
format(String,sizeof(String),"~y~~H~очки ~r~~H~%d",PlayerScore[Player]);
TextDrawSetString(ServerTextDrawFour[Player],String);
format(String,sizeof(String),"~b~~H~x%d",PlayerCombo[Player]);
TextDrawSetString(ServerTextDrawFive[Player],String);
KillTimer(PlayerTimerOne[Player]);
PlayerTimerOne[Player] = SetTimerEx("PlayerDriftEnd",3700,0,"d",Player);
}
}
}
return 1;
}
forward PlayerDriftEnd(Player);
public PlayerDriftEnd(Player)
{
TextDrawHideForPlayer(Player,ServerTextDrawThree[Player]);
TextDrawHideForPlayer(Player,ServerTextDrawFour[Player]);
TextDrawHideForPlayer(Player,ServerTextDrawFive[Player]);
TextDrawSetString(ServerTextDrawThree[Player]," ");
TextDrawSetString(ServerTextDrawFour[Player]," ");
TextDrawSetString(ServerTextDrawFive[Player]," ");
SetPVarInt(Player, "MonControl", 1);
GGivePlayerMoney(Player,PlayerMoney[Player]);
SetPVarInt(Player, "ScorControl", 3);
SetPlayerScore(Player,GetPlayerScore(Player) + PlayerScore[Player] * PlayerCombo[Player]);
PlayerMoney[Player] = 0;
PlayerScore[Player] = 0;
PlayerCombo[Player] = 1;
return 1;
}

forward MinServ();
public MinServ()
{
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
{
PlayerInfo[i][pMinlog]++;
}
}
gettime(timedata[0], timedata[1]);
if(oldhour != timedata[0])
{
oldhour = timedata[0];
}

if(timedata[0] == 3 && timedata[1] == 35) // Если 1 час 25 минут (Можно заменить время на свое)
{
SendClientMessageToAll(0x00FFFFFF, "BOBBBO SERVER :   Шановнi гравцi, через 5 хвилин сервер перезавантажиться");// Выводим сообщение в общий чат
}
if(timedata[0] == 3 && timedata[1] == 40) // Если 1 час 30 минут (Можно заменить время на свое)
{
SendClientMessageToAll(0x00FFFFFF, "Активовано автоматичний рестарт сервера ...");// Выводим сообщение в общий чат
restart = SetTimer("RestartS", 5000, 1); // Делаем рестарт
}
return 1;
}
stock ProxDetector(Float:radi, playerid, str[],col1,col2,col3,col4,col5)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(playerid))
{
new Float:posx, Float:posy, Float:posz;
new Float:oldposx, Float:oldposy, Float:oldposz;
new Float:tempposx, Float:tempposy, Float:tempposz;
GetPlayerPos(playerid, oldposx, oldposy, oldposz);
//radi = 2.0; //Trigger Radius
for(new i; i < GetMaxPlayers(); i++)
{
if(IsPlayerConnected(i))
{

GetPlayerPos(i, posx, posy, posz);
tempposx = (oldposx -posx);
tempposy = (oldposy -posy);
tempposz = (oldposz -posz);
//printf("DEBUG: X:%f Y:%f Z:%f",posx,posy,posz);
if (((tempposx < radi/16) && (tempposx > -radi/16)) && ((tempposy < radi/16) && (tempposy > -radi/16)) && ((tempposz < radi/16) && (tempposz > -radi/16)))
{
SendClientMessage(i, col1, str);
}
else if (((tempposx < radi/8) && (tempposx > -radi/8)) && ((tempposy < radi/8) && (tempposy > -radi/8)) && ((tempposz < radi/8) && (tempposz > -radi/8)))
{
SendClientMessage(i, col2, str);
}
else if (((tempposx < radi/4) && (tempposx > -radi/4)) && ((tempposy < radi/4) && (tempposy > -radi/4)) && ((tempposz < radi/4) && (tempposz > -radi/4)))
{
SendClientMessage(i, col3, str);
}
else if (((tempposx < radi/2) && (tempposx > -radi/2)) && ((tempposy < radi/2) && (tempposy > -radi/2)) && ((tempposz < radi/2) && (tempposz > -radi/2)))
{
SendClientMessage(i, col4, str);
}
else if (((tempposx < radi) && (tempposx > -radi)) && ((tempposy < radi) && (tempposy > -radi)) && ((tempposz < radi) && (tempposz > -radi)))
{
SendClientMessage(i, col5, str);
}
}
}
}
return 1;
}

stock SpeedometrVehicle(playerid)
{
new Float:ST[4];
if(IsPlayerInAnyVehicle(playerid))
GetVehicleVelocity(GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid),ST[0],ST[1],ST[2]);
else GetPlayerVelocity(playerid,ST[0],ST[1],ST[2]);
ST[3] = floatsqroot(floatpower(floatabs(ST[0]), 2.0) + floatpower(floatabs(ST[1]), 2.0) + floatpower(floatabs(ST[2]), 2.0)) * 169.5;
return floatround(ST[3]);
}

TextDrawSetString(Speedometr[playerid][2], string);
}

stock GetDistanceBetweenPlayers(playerid, playerid2)
{
new Float:x1,Float:y1,Float:z1,Float:x2,Float:y2,Float:z2;
new Float:tmpdis;
GetPlayerPos(playerid,x1,y1,z1);
GetPlayerPos(playerid2,x2,y2,z2);
tmpdis = floatsqroot(floatpower(floatabs(floatsub(x2,x1)),2)+floatpower(floatabs(floatsub(y2,y1)),2)+floatpower(floatabs(floatsub(z2,z1)),2));
return floatround(tmpdis);
}
forward split(const strsrc[], strdest[][], delimiter);
public split(const strsrc[], strdest[][], delimiter)
{
new i, li;
new aNum;
new len;
while(i <= strlen(strsrc)){
if(strsrc[i]==delimiter || i==strlen(strsrc)){
len = strmid(strdest[aNum], strsrc, li, i, 128);
strdest[aNum][len] = 0;
li = i+1;
aNum++;
}
i++;
}
return 1;
}

}
return 1;
}

forward CheckKeyPress(playerid);
public CheckKeyPress(playerid)
{
if(wait[playerid] == 0)
{
new keys, updown, leftright;
GetPlayerKeys(playerid, keys, updown, leftright);
if(leftright == KEY_RIGHT)
{
if(IsInShop[playerid] == 1)
{
skincount[playerid]++;
if(skincount[playerid] > TotalSkins)
{
skincount[playerid] = 0;
}
SetPlayerSkin(playerid, AvailableSkins[skincount[playerid]]);
wait[playerid] = 1;
SetTimerEx("ResetWait", 90, 0, "i", playerid);
format(TextDrawString[playerid], 128, "~y~кнопки ~<~ ~>~ ~y~гортати   ~n~~y~натисни ~r~ENTER ~y~шоб обрати~n~~y~(%d/%d)", skincount[playerid]+1, TotalSkins);
ApplyAnimation(playerid,"DANCING", "dnce_M_a",9.9,9,9,9,9,9);
TextDrawHideForPlayer(playerid, TextDraw[playerid]);
TextdrawActive[playerid] = 0;
TextDrawSetString(TextDraw[playerid], TextDrawString[playerid]);
TextDrawShowForPlayer(playerid, TextDraw[playerid]);
TextdrawActive[playerid] = 1;
}
}
if(leftright == KEY_LEFT)
{
if(IsInShop[playerid] == 1)
{
skincount[playerid]--;
if(skincount[playerid] == -1)
{
skincount[playerid] = TotalSkins;
}
SetPlayerSkin(playerid, AvailableSkins[skincount[playerid]]);
wait[playerid] = 1;
SetTimerEx("ResetWait", 90, 0, "i", playerid);
format(TextDrawString[playerid], 128, "~y~кнопки ~<~ ~>~ ~y~гортати   ~n~~y~натисни ~r~ENTER ~y~шоб обрати~n~~y~(%d/%d)", skincount[playerid]+1, TotalSkins);
ApplyAnimation(playerid,"DANCING", "dnce_M_a",9.9,9,9,9,9,9);
TextDrawHideForPlayer(playerid, TextDraw[playerid]);
TextdrawActive[playerid] = 0;
TextDrawSetString(TextDraw[playerid], TextDrawString[playerid]);
TextDrawShowForPlayer(playerid, TextDraw[playerid]);
TextdrawActive[playerid] = 1;
}
}
}
}
forward ResetWait(playerid);
public ResetWait(playerid)
{
wait[playerid] = 0;
}
